You can see how we calculate our billing and distribution as it is open to the entire community. Want to be a supporter of the project click [here](mailto:avelinorun+oss@gmail.com?subject=awesome-go%3A%20project%20support).*

## Actor Model

*Libraries for building actor-based programs.*

* [Ergo](https://github.com/ergo-services/ergo) ‚≠ê 4,006 | üêõ 4 | üåê Go | üìÖ 2025-06-30 - An actor-based Framework with network transparency for creating event-driven architecture in Golang. Inspired by Erlang.
* [Goakt](https://github.com/Tochemey/goakt) ‚≠ê 260 | üêõ 1 | üåê Go | üìÖ 2025-07-02 - Fast and Distributed Actor framework using protocol buffers as message for Golang.
* [Hollywood](https://github.com/anthdm/hollywood) ‚≠ê 1,966 | üêõ 23 | üåê Go | üìÖ 2025-06-06 - Blazingly fast and light-weight Actor engine written in Golang.
* [ProtoActor](https://github.com/asynkron/protoactor-go) ‚≠ê 5,252 | üêõ 88 | üåê Go | üìÖ 2024-08-22 - Proto Actor - Ultra fast distributed actors for Go, C# and Java/Kotlin.

## Artificial Intelligence

*Libraries for building programs that leverage AI.*

* [chromem-go](https://github.com/philippgille/chromem-go) ‚≠ê 614 | üêõ 11 | üåê Go | üìÖ 2025-04-27 - Embeddable vector database for Go with Chroma-like interface and zero third-party dependencies. In-memory with optional persistence.
* [fun](https://gitlab.com/tozd/go/fun) - The simplest but powerful way to use large language models (LLMs) in Go.
* [langchaingo](https://github.com/tmc/langchaingo) ‚≠ê 7,028 | üêõ 365 | üåê Go | üìÖ 2025-06-29 - LangChainGo is a framework for developing applications powered by language models.
* [LocalAI](https://github.com/mudler/LocalAI) ‚≠ê 33,631 | üêõ 481 | üåê Go | üìÖ 2025-07-02 - Open Source OpenAI alternative, self-host AI models.
* [Ollama](https://github.com/jmorganca/ollama) ‚≠ê 145,368 | üêõ 1,903 | üåê Go | üìÖ 2025-07-02 - Run large language models locally.
* [OllamaFarm](https://github.com/presbrey/ollamafarm) ‚≠ê 79 | üêõ 0 | üåê Go | üìÖ 2025-02-01 - Manage, load-balance, and failover packs of Ollamas

## Audio and Music

* [gaad](https://github.com/Comcast/gaad) ‚≠ê 129 | üêõ 2 | üåê Go | üìÖ 2023-01-27 - Native Go AAC bitstream parser.
* [GoAudio](https://github.com/DylanMeeus/GoAudio) ‚≠ê 377 | üêõ 10 | üåê Go | üìÖ 2024-04-23 - Native Go Audio Processing Library.
* [gosamplerate](https://github.com/dh1tw/gosamplerate) ‚≠ê 35 | üêõ 0 | üåê Go | üìÖ 2024-01-28 - libsamplerate bindings for go.
* [id3v2](https://github.com/bogem/id3v2) ‚≠ê 347 | üêõ 24 | üåê Go | üìÖ 2023-10-28 - ID3 decoding and encoding library for Go.
* [malgo](https://github.com/gen2brain/malgo) ‚≠ê 335 | üêõ 9 | üåê C | üìÖ 2024-10-22 - Mini audio library.
* [minimp3](https://github.com/tosone/minimp3) ‚≠ê 129 | üêõ 0 | üåê C | üìÖ 2023-08-02 - Lightweight MP3 decoder library.
* [Oto](https://github.com/hajimehoshi/oto) ‚≠ê 1,731 | üêõ 24 | üåê Go | üìÖ 2025-06-27 - A low-level library to play sound on multiple platforms.
* [PortAudio](https://github.com/gordonklaus/portaudio) ‚≠ê 776 | üêõ 6 | üåê Go | üìÖ 2025-02-06 - Go bindings for the PortAudio audio I/O library.

## Authentication and OAuth

*Libraries for implementing authentication schemes.*

* [authboss](https://github.com/volatiletech/authboss) ‚≠ê 3,987 | üêõ 41 | üåê Go | üìÖ 2025-06-26 - Modular authentication system for the web. It tries to remove as much boilerplate and "hard things" as possible so that each time you start a new web project in Go, you can plug it in, configure it, and start building your app without having to build an authentication system each time.
* [branca](https://github.com/essentialkaos/branca) ‚≠ê 90 | üêõ 0 | üåê Go | üìÖ 2025-06-17 - branca token [specification implementation](https://github.com/tuupola/branca-spec) ‚≠ê 230 | üêõ 10 | üìÖ 2025-05-06 for Golang 1.15+.
* [casbin](https://github.com/hsluoyz/casbin) ‚≠ê 18,818 | üêõ 48 | üåê Go | üìÖ 2025-06-21 - Authorization library that supports access control models like ACL, RBAC, and ABAC.
* [cookiestxt](https://github.com/mengzhuo/cookiestxt) ‚≠ê 19 | üêõ 0 | üåê Go | üìÖ 2024-03-12 - provides a parser of cookies.txt file format.
* [go-guardian](https://github.com/shaj13/go-guardian) ‚≠ê 588 | üêõ 12 | üåê Go | üìÖ 2024-07-25 - Go-Guardian is a golang library that provides a simple, clean, and idiomatic way to create powerful modern API and web authentication that supports LDAP, Basic, Bearer token, and Certificate based authentication.
* [go-jose](https://github.com/go-jose/go-jose) ‚≠ê 413 | üêõ 31 | üåê Go | üìÖ 2025-06-26 - Fairly complete implementation of the JOSE working group's JSON Web Token, JSON Web Signatures, and JSON Web Encryption specs.
* [goiabada](https://github.com/leodip/goiabada) ‚≠ê 154 | üêõ 5 | üåê Go | üìÖ 2025-02-24 - An open-source authentication and authorization server supporting OAuth2 and OpenID Connect.
* [gologin](https://github.com/dghubble/gologin) ‚≠ê 1,914 | üêõ 0 | üåê Go | üìÖ 2025-07-02 - chainable handlers for login with OAuth1 and OAuth2 authentication providers.
* [gorbac](https://github.com/mikespook/gorbac) ‚≠ê 1,632 | üêõ 4 | üåê Go | üìÖ 2024-07-22 - provides a lightweight role-based access control (RBAC) implementation in Golang.
* [gosession](https://github.com/Kwynto/gosession) ‚≠ê 258 | üêõ 0 | üåê Go | üìÖ 2024-07-31 - This is quick session for net/http in GoLang. This package is perhaps the best implementation of the session mechanism, or at least it tries to become one.
* [goth](https://github.com/markbates/goth) ‚≠ê 6,074 | üêõ 132 | üåê Go | üìÖ 2025-04-04 - provides a simple, clean, and idiomatic way to use OAuth and OAuth2. Handles multiple providers out of the box.
* [jeff](https://github.com/abraithwaite/jeff) ‚≠ê 269 | üêõ 2 | üåê Go | üìÖ 2025-01-23 - Simple, flexible, secure, and idiomatic web session management with pluggable backends.
* [jwt](https://github.com/pascaldekloe/jwt) ‚≠ê 362 | üêõ 0 | üåê Go | üìÖ 2023-04-29 - Lightweight JSON Web Token (JWT) library.
* [jwt](https://github.com/cristalhq/jwt) ‚≠ê 685 | üêõ 2 | üåê Go | üìÖ 2025-06-22 - Safe, simple, and fast JSON Web Tokens for Go.
* [jwt-auth](https://github.com/adam-hanna/jwt-auth) ‚≠ê 234 | üêõ 4 | üåê Go | üìÖ 2021-08-01 - JWT middleware for Golang http servers with many configuration options.
* [jwt-go](https://github.com/golang-jwt/jwt) ‚≠ê 8,213 | üêõ 46 | üåê Go | üìÖ 2025-07-01 - A full featured implementation of JSON Web Tokens (JWT). This library supports the parsing and verification as well as the generation and signing of JWTs.
* [jwx](https://github.com/lestrrat-go/jwx) ‚≠ê 2,127 | üêõ 4 | üåê Go | üìÖ 2025-07-03 - Go module implementing various JWx (JWA/JWE/JWK/JWS/JWT, otherwise known as JOSE) technologies
* [keto](https://github.com/ory/keto) ‚≠ê 5,053 | üêõ 59 | üåê Go | üìÖ 2025-07-02 - Open Source (Go) implementation of "Zanzibar: Google's Consistent, Global Authorization System". Ships gRPC, REST APIs, newSQL, and an easy and granular permission language. Supports ACL, RBAC, and other access models.
* [loginsrv](https://github.com/tarent/loginsrv) ‚≠ê 1,925 | üêõ 28 | üåê Go | üìÖ 2021-02-27 - JWT login microservice with pluggable backends such as OAuth2 (Github), htpasswd, osiam.
* [oauth2](https://github.com/golang/oauth2) ‚≠ê 5,638 | üêõ 39 | üåê Go | üìÖ 2025-05-05 - Successor of goauth2. Generic OAuth 2.0 package that comes with JWT, Google APIs, Compute Engine, and App Engine support.
* [oidc](https://github.com/zitadel/oidc) ‚≠ê 1,598 | üêõ 30 | üåê Go | üìÖ 2025-07-02 - Easy to use OpenID Connect client and server library written for Go and certified by the OpenID Foundation
* [openfga](https://github.com/openfga/openfga) ‚≠ê 3,776 | üêõ 129 | üåê Go | üìÖ 2025-07-02 - Implementation of fine-grained authorization based on the "Zanzibar: Google's Consistent, Global Authorization System" paper. Backed by [CNCF](https://www.cncf.io/).
* [osin](https://github.com/openshift/osin) ‚≠ê 1,927 | üêõ 3 | üåê Go | üìÖ 2025-05-08 - Golang OAuth2 server library.
* [otpgen](https://github.com/grijul/otpgen) ‚≠ê 139 | üêõ 1 | üåê Go | üìÖ 2024-01-17 - Library to generate TOTP/HOTP codes.
* [otpgo](https://github.com/jltorresm/otpgo) ‚≠ê 75 | üêõ 2 | üåê Go | üìÖ 2021-02-27 - Time-Based One-Time Password (TOTP) and HMAC-Based One-Time Password (HOTP) library for Go.
* [paseto](https://github.com/o1egl/paseto) ‚≠ê 897 | üêõ 6 | üåê Go | üìÖ 2023-02-25 - Golang implementation of Platform-Agnostic Security Tokens (PASETO).
* [permissions](https://github.com/xyproto/permissions) ‚≠ê 9 | üêõ 0 | üåê Go | üìÖ 2024-12-01 - Library for keeping track of users, login states, and permissions. Uses secure cookies and bcrypt.
* [scope](https://github.com/SonicRoshan/scope) ‚≠ê 41 | üêõ 1 | üåê Go | üìÖ 2021-05-25 - Easily Manage OAuth2 Scopes In Go.
* [scs](https://github.com/alexedwards/scs) ‚≠ê 2,352 | üêõ 29 | üåê Go | üìÖ 2025-04-17 - Session Manager for HTTP servers.
* [securecookie](https://github.com/chmike/securecookie) ‚≠ê 81 | üêõ 0 | üåê Go | üìÖ 2023-02-18 - Efficient secure cookie encoding/decoding.
* [session](https://github.com/icza/session) ‚≠ê 118 | üêõ 4 | üåê Go | üìÖ 2024-08-24 - Go session management for web servers (including support for Google App Engine - GAE).
* [sessions](https://github.com/adam-hanna/sessions) ‚≠ê 78 | üêõ 4 | üåê Go | üìÖ 2023-07-17 - Dead simple, highly performant, highly customizable sessions service for go http servers.
* [sessionup](https://github.com/swithek/sessionup) ‚≠ê 127 | üêõ 3 | üåê Go | üìÖ 2025-03-20 - Simple, yet effective HTTP session management and identification package.
* [sjwt](https://github.com/brianvoe/sjwt) ‚≠ê 122 | üêõ 1 | üåê Go | üìÖ 2024-02-01 - Simple jwt generator and parser.
* [x509proxy](https://github.com/vkuznet/x509proxy) ‚≠ê 6 | üêõ 0 | üåê Go | üìÖ 2025-01-19 - Library to handle X509 proxy certificates.

## Blockchain

*Tools for building blockchains.*

* [cometbft](https://github.com/cometbft/cometbft) ‚≠ê 758 | üêõ 272 | üåê Go | üìÖ 2025-07-02 - A distributed, Byzantine fault-tolerant, deterministic state machine replication engine. It is a fork of Tendermint Core and implements the Tendermint consensus algorithm.
* [cosmos-sdk](https://github.com/cosmos/cosmos-sdk) ‚≠ê 6,637 | üêõ 272 | üåê Go | üìÖ 2025-07-02 - A Framework for Building Public Blockchains in the Cosmos Ecosystem.
* [gno](https://github.com/gnolang/gno) ‚≠ê 972 | üêõ 800 | üåê Go | üìÖ 2025-07-03 - A comprehensive smart contract suite built with Golang and Gnolang, a deterministic, purpose-built Go variant for blockchains.

### Bloom and Cuckoo Filters

* [bloom](https://github.com/bits-and-blooms/bloom) ‚≠ê 2,617 | üêõ 18 | üåê Go | üìÖ 2024-12-10 - Go package implementing Bloom filters.

## Package Management

*Official tooling for dependency and package management*

* [go modules](https://golang.org/cmd/go/#hdr-Modules__module_versions__and_more) - Modules are the unit of source code interchange and versioning. The go command has direct support for working with modules, including recording and resolving dependencies on other modules.

## Benchmarks

* [autobench](https://github.com/davecheney/autobench) ‚≠ê 99 | üêõ 2 | üåê Go | üìÖ 2014-07-28 - Framework to compare the performance between different Go versions.
* [go-benchmark-app](https://github.com/mrLSD/go-benchmark-app) ‚≠ê 28 | üêõ 0 | üåê Go | üìÖ 2017-03-17 - Powerful HTTP-benchmark tool mixed with –êb, Wrk, Siege tools. Gathering statistics and various parameters for benchmarks and comparison results.
* [go-benchmarks](https://github.com/tylertreat/go-benchmarks) ‚≠ê 148 | üêõ 2 | üåê Go | üìÖ 2016-02-25 - Few miscellaneous Go microbenchmarks. Compare some language features to alternative approaches.

### E-books for purchase

* [Go in Practice, Second Edition](https://www.manning.com/books/go-in-practice-second-edition)  - Your practical guide on the ins-and-outs of Go development, covering the standard library and the most important tools from Go‚Äôs powerful ecosystem.

* [Lets-Go](https://lets-go.alexedwards.net) - A step-by-step guide to creating fast, secure and maintanable web applications with Go.
* [Lets-Go-Further](https://lets-go-further.alexedwards.net) - Advanced patterns for building APIs and web applications in Go.
* [The Power of Go: Tests](https://bitfieldconsulting.com/books/tests) - A guide to testing in Go.
* [The Power of Go: Tools](https://bitfieldconsulting.com/books/tools) - A guide to writing command-line tools in Go.
* [Writing A Compiler In Go](https://compilerbook.com)
* [Writing An Interpreter In Go](https://interpreterbook.com) - Book that introduces dozens of techniques for writing idiomatic, expressive, and efficient Go code that avoids common pitfalls.
